# Fix UDP Proxy Crash on Dynamic CDS/EDS Cluster Updates

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/envoy--1ae957c1 (mirror of envoyproxy/envoy)
**Difficulty:** MEDIUM
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix

## Description

Envoy's UDP proxy filter crashes when a pre-existing cluster is updated via CDS (Cluster Discovery Service), for example when `HostSet` changes occur. The crash happens because `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` in `udp_proxy_filter.cc` uses `std::unordered_map::emplace()` to insert cluster info into the `cluster_infos_` map.

When a cluster with the same name already exists (i.e., it's being updated rather than added for the first time), `emplace()` silently fails — it returns the existing entry unchanged without inserting the new one. This leaves a stale `ClusterInfo` object in the map that references the old `ThreadLocalCluster`. When the old `ThreadLocalCluster` is destroyed as part of the update, the filter still holds a dangling pointer through the stale map entry, leading to a crash on the next packet.

The fix replaces `emplace()` with `insert_or_assign()` in both the per-packet-load-balancing and sticky-session code paths, so that cluster updates correctly replace the old entry.

## Task

Changes:
- 3 files modified (changelogs/current.yaml, udp_proxy_filter.cc, udp_proxy_filter_test.cc)
- 52 additions, 4 deletions

Tasks:
1. Fix `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` in `source/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter.cc` to use `insert_or_assign()` instead of `emplace()` in both code paths
2. Add a regression test `ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate` in the UDP proxy filter test file
3. Add a changelog entry in `changelogs/current.yaml` under `bug_fixes`

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 3 modified files updated correctly.

    43→void UdpProxyFilter::onClusterAddOrUpdate(absl::string_view cluster_name,
    44→                                          Upstream::ThreadLocalClusterCommand& get_cluster) {
    45→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, "udp proxy: attaching to cluster {}", cluster_name);
    46→
    47→  auto& cluster = get_cluster();
    48→  ASSERT((!cluster_infos_.contains(cluster_name)) ||
    49→         &cluster_infos_[cluster_name]->cluster_ != &cluster);
    50→
    51→  if (config_->usingPerPacketLoadBalancing()) {
    52→    cluster_infos_.emplace(cluster_name,
    53→                           std::make_unique<PerPacketLoadBalancingClusterInfo>(*this, cluster));
    54→  } else {
    55→    cluster_infos_.emplace(cluster_name,
    56→                           std::make_unique<StickySessionClusterInfo>(*this, cluster));
    57→  }
    58→}

    44→                                          Upstream::ThreadLocalClusterCommand& get_cluster) {
    45→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, "udp proxy: attaching to cluster {}", cluster_name);

    48→  ASSERT((!cluster_infos_.contains(cluster_name)) ||
    49→         &cluster_infos_[cluster_name]->cluster_ != &cluster);

103-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully completed all three required tasks to fix the UDP proxy crash on dynamic CDS/EDS cluster updates:

## Summary of Changes

### 1. **Fixed `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` in `udp_proxy_filter.cc`**
- **Line 52**: Changed `cluster_infos_.emplace()` → `cluster_infos_.insert_or_assign()` for per-packet load balancing code path
- **Line 55**: Changed `cluster_infos_.emplace()` → `cluster_infos_.insert_or_assign()` for sticky session code path

**Why this fix works:** 
- `emplace()` silently fails when the key already exists, leaving a stale reference to the old cluster
- `insert_or_assign()` correctly replaces the existing entry with the new cluster info, preventing dangling pointers when the old cluster is destroyed

### 2. **Added regression test `ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate`**
- Located at line 1576 in `udp_proxy_filter_test.cc`
- Tests that calling `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` with the same cluster name twice correctly updates the cluster info map
- Verifies the filter still works correctly after a cluster update by creating a new session
- Includes detailed comments explaining the regression scenario

### 3. **Added changelog entry in `changelogs/current.yaml`**
- Added under `bug_fixes` section with `area: udp`
- Documents the fix for the crash when pre-existing clusters are updated via CDS
- Explains both the problem (silently ignoring updates) and the solution (correct replacement)

## Files Modified
- `source/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter.cc` (2 lines changed)
- `test/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter_test.cc` (48 lines added)
- `changelogs/current.yaml` (5 lines added)

All changes follow Envoy conventions and are minimal, focused implementations addressing the exact issue described.

EXPECT_CALL(*idle_timer_, enableTimer(parent_.config_->sessionTimeout(), nullptr));\n\n      if (parent_.expect_gro_) {\n        EXPECT_CALL(*socket_->io_handle_, supportsUdpGro());\n      }\n Invoke([this, data, recv_sys_errno](\n                         Buffer::RawSlice* slices, const uint64_t, uint32_t,\n                         Network::IoHandle::RecvMsgOutput& output) -> Api::IoCallUint64Result {\n                if (recv_sys_errno != 0) {\n                  return makeError(recv_sys_errno);\n                } else {\n                  ASSERT(data.size() <= slices[0].len_);\n                  memcpy(slices[0].mem_, data.data(), data.size());\n                  output.msg_[0].peer_address_ = upstream_address_;\n                  return makeNoError(data.size());\n                }\n              }));\n      if (recv_sys_errno == 0) {\n        // Send the datagram downstream.\n        EXPECT_CALL(parent_.callbacks_.udp_listener_, send(_))\n            .WillOnce(Invoke([data, send_sys_errno](\n                                 const Network::UdpSendData& send_data) -> Api::IoCallUint64Result {\n              // TODO(mattklein123): Verify peer/local address.\n              EXPECT_EQ(send_data.buffer_.toString(), data);\n              if (send_sys_errno == 0) {\n                send_data.buffer_.drain(send_data.buffer_.length());\n                return makeNoError(data.size());\n              } else {\n                return makeError(send_sys_errno);\n              }\n            }));\n        // Return an EAGAIN result.\n        EXPECT_CALL(*socket_->io_handle_, recvmsg(_, 1, _, _))\n            .WillOnce(Return(ByMove(\n                Api::IoCallUint64Result(0, Network::IoSocketError::getIoSocketEagainError()))));\n      }\n\n      // Kick off the receive.\n      file_event_cb_(Event::FileReadyType::Read);\n    }\n\n    UdpProxyFilterTest& parent_;\n    const Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr upstream_address_;\n    Event::MockTimer* idle_timer_{};\n    NiceMock<Network::MockSocket>* socket_;\n    std::map<int, std::map<int, int>> sock_opts_;\n    Event::FileReadyCb file_event_cb_;\n  };\n\n  UdpProxyFilterTest()\n      : UdpProxyFilterTest(Network::Utility::parseInternetAddressAndPort(peer_ip_address_)) {}\n\n  explicit UdpProxyFilterTest(Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr&& peer_address)\n      : os_calls_(&os_sys_calls_),\n        upstream_address_(Network::Utility::parseInternetAddressAndPort(upstream_ip_address_)),\n        peer_address_(std::move(peer_address)) {\n    // Disable strict mock warnings.\n    ON_CALL(*factory_context_.server_factory_context_.access_log_manager_.file_, write(_))\n        .WillByDefault(\n            Invoke([&](absl::string_view data) { output_.push_back(std::string(data)); }));\n    ON_CALL(os_sys_calls_, supportsIpTransparent(_)).WillByDefault(Return(true));\n    EXPECT_CALL(os_sys_calls_, supportsUdpGro()).Times(AtLeast(0)).WillRepeatedly(Return(true));\n    EXPECT_CALL(callbacks_, udpListener()).Times(AtLeast(0));\n    EXPECT_CALL(\n        *factory_context_.server_factory_context_.cluster_manager_.thread_local_cluster_.lb_.host_,\n        address())\n        .WillRepeatedly(Return(upstream_address_));\n    EXPECT_CALL(\n        *factory_context_.server_factory_context_.cluster_manager_.thread_local_cluster_.lb_.host_,\n        coarseHealth())\n        .WillRepeatedly(Return(Upstream::Host::Health::Healthy));\n  }\n\n  ~UdpProxyFilterTest() override { EXPECT_CALL(callbacks_.udp_listener_, onDestroy()); }\n\n  void setup(const envoy::extensions::filters::udp::udp_proxy::v3::UdpProxyConfig& config,\n             bool has_cluster = true, bool expect_gro = true) {\n    config_ = Network::Utility::parseInternetAddressAndPort(local_address);\n    data.buffer_ = std::make_unique<Buffer::OwnedImpl>(buffer);\n    data.receive_time_ = MonotonicTime(std::chrono::seconds(0));\n    filter_->onData(data);\n  }\n\n  void expectSessionCreate(const Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr& address) {\n    test_sessions_.emplace_back(*this, address);\n    TestSession& new_session = EXPECT_EQ(output_.back(), \"fake_cluster 0 10 1 0 2\");\n}\n\n// Verify upstream connect error handling.\nTEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ConnectErrorHandling) {\n  InSequence s;\n\n  const std::string When the headers are normalized to H1, the method\n    // is replaced with GET, a header with the 'upgrade' key is added with 'connect-udp'\n    // value and a header with the 'connection' key is added with 'Upgrade' value.\n    std::string scheme = is_ssl ? \"https\" : \"http\";\n    std::string authority =\n        opt_authority.has_value() ? opt_authority.value() : \"Upgrade\");\n    }\n\n    if (header_to_add) {\n      headers.addCopy(header_to_add.value().key_, header_to_add.value().value_);\n    }\n\n    return headers;\n  }\n\n  void true);\n  recvDataFromDownstream(\"10.0.0.1:1001\", \"10.0.0.2:80\", \"world\");\n}\n\nclass HttpUpstreamImplTest : public testing::Test {\npublic:\n  struct HeaderToAdd {\n    std::string key_;\n    std::string value_;\n  };\n\n  Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl\n  expectedHeaders(bool is_ssl = false, bool use_post = false,\n                  absl::optional<std::string> opt_authority = absl::nullopt,\n                  absl::optional<std::string> opt_path = absl::nullopt,\n                  absl::optional<HeaderToAdd> header_to_add = absl::nullopt) {\n    // In case connect-udp is used, Envoy expect the H2 headers to be normalized with H1,\n    // so expect that the request headers here match H1 headers, even though\n    // eventually H2 headers will be sent. When the headers are normalized to H1, the method\n    // is replaced with GET, a header with the 'upgrade' key is added with 'connect-udp'\n    // value and a header with the 'connection' key is added with 'Upgrade' value.\n    std::string scheme = is_ssl ? \"https\" : \"http\";\n    std::string authority =\n        opt_authority.has_value() ? opt_authority.value() : \"default.host.com:10\";\n    std::string method = use_post ? \"POST\" : \"GET\";\n    std::string path =\n        opt_path.has_value() ? opt_path.value() : \"/.well-known/masque/udp/default.target.host/20/\";\n\n    auto headers = Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl{\n        {\":scheme\", scheme}, {\":authority\", authority}, {\":method\", method}, {\":path\", path}};\n\n    if (!use_post) {\n      headers.addCopy(\"capsule-protocol\", \"?1\");\n      headers.addCopy(\"upgrade\", \"connect-udp\");\n      headers.addCopy(\"connection\", \"Upgrade\");\n    }\n\n    if (header_to_add) {\n      headers.addCopy(header_to_add.value().key_, header_to_add.value().value_);\n    }\n\n    return headers;\n  }\n\n  void setAndExpectRequestEncoder(Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl expected_headers,\n                                  bool is_ssl = false) {\n    EXPECT_CALL(request_encoder_.stream_, addCallbacks(_));\n    EXPECT_CALL(request_encoder_, encodeHeaders(_, _))\n        .WillOnce(Invoke([expected_headers](const Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers,\n                                            bool end_stream) -> Http::Status {\n          EXPECT_THAT(&headers, HeaderMapEqualIgnoreOrder(&expected_headers));\n          EXPECT_FALSE(end_stream);\n          return absl::OkStatus();\n        }));\n\n    upstream_->setRequestEncoder(request_encoder_, is_ssl);\n\n    // Verify that resetEncoder is called only once.\n    EXPECT_CALL(request_encoder_.stream_, removeCallbacks(_));\n  }\n\n  void filterStateOverride(absl::optional<uint32_t> proxy_port = absl::nullopt,\n                           absl::optional<uint32_t> target_port = absl::nullopt) {\n    if (proxy_port) {\n      stream_info_.filterState()->setData(\n          \"udp.connect.proxy_port\",\n          std::make_shared<StreamInfo::UInt32AccessorImpl>(proxy_port.value()),\n          Envoy::StreamInfo::FilterState::StateType::Mutable);\n    }\n\n    if (target_port) {\n      stream_info_.filterState()->setData(\n          \"udp.connect.target_port\",\n          std::make_shared<StreamInfo::UInt32AccessorImpl>(target_port.value()),\n          Envoy::StreamInfo::FilterState::StateType::Mutable);\n    }\n  }\n\n  void setup(absl::optional<HeaderToAdd> header_to_add = absl::nullopt) {\n    Protobuf::RepeatedPtrField<envoy::config::core::v3::HeaderValueOption> headers_to_add;\n    if (header_to_add) {\n      envoy::config::core::v3::HeaderValueOption* header = headers_to_add.Add();\n      header->mutable_header()->set_key(header_to_add.value().key_);\n      header->mutable_header()->set_value(header_to_add.value().value_);\n    }\n\n    header_evaluator_ = Envoy::Router::HeaderParser::configure(headers_to_add);\n    config_ = std::make_unique<NiceMock<MockUdpTunnelingConfig>>(*header_evaluator_);\n    upstream_ = std::make_unique<HttpUpstreamImpl>(callbacks_, *config_, stream_info_);\n    upstream_->setTunnelCreationCallbacks(creation_callbacks_);\n  }\n\n  NiceMock<MockUpstreamTunnelCallbacks> callbacks_;\n  NiceMock<StreamInfo::MockStreamInfo> stream_info_;\n // Test that cluster updates correctly replace old cluster info in the info map.
TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate) {
  InSequence s;

  setup(readConfig(R"EOF(
stat_prefix: foo
matcher:
  on_no_match:
    action:
      name: route
      typed_config:
        '@type': type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.udp.udp_proxy.v3.Route
        cluster: fake_cluster
  )EOF"));

  // Create a session with the initial cluster.
  expectSessionCreate(upstream_address_);
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("hello", 0, nullptr, true);

// Test that cluster updates correctly replace old cluster info in the info map.
// This is a regression test for https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/XXXXX
// where emplace() would silently fail when updating an existing cluster.
TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate) {
  InSequence s;

  setup(readConfig(R"EOF(
stat_prefix: foo
matcher:
  on_no_match:
    action:
      name: route
      typed_config:
        '@type': type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.udp.udp_proxy.v3.Route
        cluster: fake_cluster
  )EOF"));

  // Create a session with the initial cluster.
  expectSessionCreate(upstream_address_);
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("hello", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "hello");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_total_.value());
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());

  // Simulate a cluster update by calling onClusterAddOrUpdate again with the same
  // cluster name. This can happen during dynamic cluster updates (e.g., HostSet changes).
  // With the old code using emplace(), this would fail silently and leave a stale
  // ClusterInfo pointing to the old ThreadLocalCluster. With insert_or_assign(), the
  // old entry is correctly replaced.
  {
    Upstream::ThreadLocalClusterCommand command = [this]() -> Upstream::ThreadLocalCluster& {
      return factory_context_.server_factory_context_.cluster_manager_.thread_local_cluster_;
    };
    cluster_update_callbacks_->onClusterAddOrUpdate(
        factory_context_.server_factory_context_.cluster_manager_.thread_local_cluster_.info()
            ->name(),
        command);
  }

  // After the update, verify that the filter still works correctly and a new session
  // can be created withou
